< Review>
If you're in Sacramento when the Steelers are playing and you need a Steelers bar, look no further that Cheaters Sports Bar. I know, I know, from the name it sounds like a Patriots bar, but the inflatable Steelers helmet outside welcomes you in. You'll know you're in the right place. The other Steelers fans there will invite you in like family. Almost want my home town Steelers family to make a trip up here and party with them! Thank you Sacramento Steelers family and Cheaters Sports Bar!<//Review>

They worked quickly and efficiently and did an excellent job boxing up a few loose things that I failed to get into boxes.  Everything arrived in perfect shape.  The ground was wet and they took great care to keep the carpet clean at the target apartment.  Moving is stressful; these guys made it smooth.  The lady who did the booking out of L.A. was efficient and gracious.  I recommend this company.<//text>

< text>
Our OOB movers helped us move from NorCal to SoCal. What should have been a easy 4-hour pack ended up taking 8-hours and a little extra space than we anticipated. Even so, we had no complaints from our two guys we had (who are actually brothers and specialize in Nor- / SoCal runs). During the unpacking, we thankfully ended up by chance with the same crew+1, and managed to unpack the truck in 2 hours. We did not want reassembly services since we had some reorganizing to do so I cannot comment on that piece of OOB. Because of the great moving experience, we felt compelled to reward each leg of the trip with extra gratuity cash tips for each person. We didn't have to, it wasn't asked or even alluded to, but it was certainly deserved. I hope to never ever move again, but if I do, I'll call OOB since the transaction was very smooth for everyone. The OOB moving price was on-par with competitors. There was actually 1 cheaper solution but in the moving chaos I forgot to call them back before signing with OOB; who knows what the experience would have been? Don't know. I do know that OOB was able to schedule my move within 4 business days, though I do not recommend that approach! I had one Ikea shelving unit break during the move, but considering the condition of CA roads for 440 miles, I was expecting a few more things to break that didn't. I know this post sounds like a planned review but it isn't. It's my one genuine experience with OOB and their crew. All the best with your move, I hope this helps.< /text>

<UserId.>117216731652204827869<//UserId.><Name>Steven Pappas</Name><time>1542916182466</time><rating>1<//rating>< text>
I am writing this on behalf of my 87 year- old great aunt who purchased a car at Sam Linder Honda on 10/26/18.

My great aunt was rear ended in her 2007 Honda CR-V and wanted to purchase another Honda since they are such reliable cars.

She was shown a 2017 Honda HR-V EX w/ navigation (top of the line model) with 3,081 miles. She ended up purchasing the car in cash, wrote a check that day and drove home in her new car. I received a call that she bought a new car and wanted me to see it, I went to her house and saw the car.

She showed me the long, yellow paper which is referred to as the sales contract. I was surprised to see that in line 1a (cost before any tax, fees, etc) that she paid $26,487.74 for the vehicle. On the Honda website the MSRP of a new 2018 model was $26,540. A new one would be $52.26 more than a year old HR-V. She also got a 7 year/75,000 mile warranty for $2,235.

I looked in the glovebox to find the manual and discovered an envelope of papers. I assumed they were my great aunt's and gave them to her. She said it was a sales contract with another persons name on it. We discovered that the woman who purchased the car new one year before left her sales contract in the car. That concerned me being that the car was certified preowned and they didn't check the glovebox, did they check everything else under the hood? Upon opening it up I saw that on line 1a she paid $25,146.00 when the car was new with 59 miles on it and only $1,845 for the same warranty. My great aunt paid $1,341.74 MORE for the exact same car than the first owner did (excluding warranty).

My father, great aunt and I called and spoke to the general sales manager, Al Feria, who was very nice and helpful.

I asked why this car cost more than a new car and he explained that the two plants that produce the EX w/ navigation were out of commission which made that particular model in high demand due to there not being a lot of them. He said that the same day my aunt purchased two other people came in looking to buy it. I looked and found a like model without AWD for $21,500 with 11,000 miles on it.

I brought up that the dealership failed to check the glovebox and left the contract in it from the old owner. The phone disconnected shortly after stating the above but Al immediately returned my call. He said that some employee was getting written up for leaving the contract in the glovebox which is unfortunate but I would be furious if my personal information was left for people to find.

He kept asking how we can fix the situation and I said take the car back. He offered us $23,000 to take the car back which would have been a huge loss in money. I told him that we would would get back to him regarding the warranty and said I was going to post this online for others to see. He then began explaining all the great things Sam Linder does for the community and that he'd take the review personally. I politely ended the call by saying that nothing else needed to be said and I was getting frustrated.

Call it what you want, but I feel that my great aunt was taken advantage of and essentially got ripped off.<//text>

<review>Been coming here for over a decade. And the food, bread, bagels still taste the same and keeps me coming back!

My favorite is the Main St. Special (Turkey & Avacado) on the parmesan bread.(Bread is always toasted before they put on anything.

Something strange happened to me at this vet hospital. I arrived at the hospital per my appointment and called from The outside in the parking lot. Staff was busy. I did not get an answer. < Text>
I got my tattoo from Mars, or cloudsolid on Instagram, and it was all around perfect.
First of all, he is overall super nice and chill. He can draw anything you suggest and he will get it exactly how you imagine it. Then throughout the whole process he makes sure you‚Äôre comfortable, relaxed and able to keep going. During the tattoo you can just chat and have a nice convo, or if you need to relax he will just focus on the tattoo and not even mind, so he is great for all those introverted snd extroverted people. He is also very nice about working with your budget. You can tell him how much you have and he will completely work around that.
Secondly, just his tattoo machine is the best because it is so quite and feels super nice compared to other tattoo machines. For me it felt the same as someone drawing on my arm with a fine tip sharpie.
Third, the atmosphere is really nice. All the artists seem really nice and welcoming. The shop feels like a place of happy times with people being hyped about their new art or just hanging out with pals.
Overall this was by far the best experience I had getting a tattoo. The tattoo turned out absolutely amazing and I had so much fun getting it done.< /Text>
